ì´ì œ Aura í”ŒëŸ¬ê·¸ì¸ì„ ë‹¤ì‹œ ë¹Œë“œí•´ì„œ ì—°ê²° ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ í•´ê²°í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

## í˜„ì¬ ìƒí™© ì •ë¦¬ ë° í•´ê²° ë°©ì•ˆ

ì§€ê¸ˆê¹Œì§€ í™•ì¸í•œ ìƒí™©:

1. âœ… **ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ì„œë²„**: ì •ìƒ ì‹¤í–‰ ì¤‘ (í¬íŠ¸ 8001)
2. â“ **ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸**: ì‹¤í–‰ ì‹œë„í–ˆì§€ë§Œ ë¡œê·¸ í™•ì¸ ì–´ë ¤ì›€
3. âŒ **Aura í”ŒëŸ¬ê·¸ì¸**: Node.js í™˜ê²½ ë¬¸ì œë¡œ ë¹Œë“œ ë¶ˆê°€
4. â“ **ì„œë²„ ë¡œê·¸**: MCP ì—°ê²°ì€ ë˜ì§€ë§Œ API í‚¤ ë¬¸ì œ ì¡´ì¬

ìš°ì„  ê°€ì¥ ì¤‘ìš”í•œ ê²ƒë¶€í„° í•´ê²°í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
ì—°ê²° ìƒíƒœ ë””ë²„ê¹… ë° í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸
"""
import requests
import json
import time
from datetime import datetime

def test_dashboard_server():
    """ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ì„œë²„ ì—°ê²° í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸"""
    print("ğŸ” ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ì„œë²„ ì—°ê²° í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸...")
    
    endpoints = [
        "/api/health",
        "/api/metrics", 
        "/api/agents/status",
        "/api/chat/history"
    ]
    
    base_url = "http://localhost:8001"
    
    for endpoint in endpoints:
        try:
            response = requests.get(f"{base_url}{endpoint}", timeout=5)
            print(f"âœ… {endpoint}: {response.status_code} - {response.text[:100]}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ {endpoint}: {str(e)}")

def test_mcp_server():
    """MCP ì„œë²„ ì—°ê²° í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸"""
    print("\nğŸ” MCP ì„œë²„ ì—°ê²° í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸...")
    
    mcp_url = "https://shrimp-mcp-production.up.railway.app"
    
    try:
        response = requests.get(mcp_url, timeout=10)
        print(f"âœ… MCP ì„œë²„: {response.status_code}")
        print(f"   ì‘ë‹µ: {response.text[:200]}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ MCP ì„œë²„: {str(e)}")

def check_agent_processes():
    """ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ í”„ë¡œì„¸ìŠ¤ í™•ì¸"""
    print("\nğŸ” ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ í”„ë¡œì„¸ìŠ¤ í™•ì¸...")
    
    import psutil
    
    python_processes = []
    for proc in psutil.process_iter(['pid', 'name', 'cmdline']):
        try:
            if 'python' in proc.info['name'].lower():
                cmdline = ' '.join(proc.info['cmdline'] or [])
                if 'super_unified_agent' in cmdline:
                    python_processes.append({
                        'pid': proc.info['pid'],
                        'cmdline': cmdline
                    })
        except (psutil.NoSuchProcess, psutil.AccessDenied):
            continue
    
    if python_processes:
        print("âœ… ë°œê²¬ëœ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ í”„ë¡œì„¸ìŠ¤:")
        for proc in python_processes:
            print(f"   PID {proc['pid']}: {proc['cmdline']}")
    else:
        print("âŒ ì‹¤í–‰ ì¤‘ì¸ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ í”„ë¡œì„¸ìŠ¤ê°€ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.")

def test_agent_startup():
    """ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì‹œì‘ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸"""
    print("\nğŸš€ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì‹œì‘ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸...")
    
    import subprocess
    import sys
    
    try:
        # ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë°±ê·¸ë¼ìš´ë“œì—ì„œ ì‹œì‘
        process = subprocess.Popen([
            sys.executable, 
            "super_unified_agent.py", 
            "super_heroic"
        ], stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE, text=True)
        
        print(f"âœ… ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ í”„ë¡œì„¸ìŠ¤ ì‹œì‘ë¨ (PID: {process.pid})")
        
        # 5ì´ˆ ëŒ€ê¸° í›„ ìƒíƒœ í™•ì¸
        time.sleep(5)
        
        if process.poll() is None:
            print("âœ… ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ê°€ ì •ìƒì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì‹¤í–‰ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.")
            return process
        else:
            stdout, stderr = process.communicate()
            print(f"âŒ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ ì‹¤íŒ¨:")
            print(f"   STDOUT: {stdout}")
            print(f"   STDERR: {stderr}")
            return None
            
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì‹œì‘ ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
        return None

def check_log_files():
    """ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ í™•ì¸"""
    print("\nğŸ“‹ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ í™•ì¸...")
    
    import os
    from pathlib import Path
    
    log_dir = Path("logs")
    if not log_dir.exists():
        print("âŒ logs ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ê°€ ì¡´ì¬í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.")
        return
    
    # ì˜¤ëŠ˜ ë‚ ì§œ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì°¾ê¸°
    today = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")
    today_logs = list(log_dir.glob(f"*{today}*"))
    
    if today_logs:
        print("âœ… ì˜¤ëŠ˜ ìƒì„±ëœ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼:")
        for log_file in today_logs:
            size = log_file.stat().st_size
            print(f"   {log_file.name}: {size} bytes")
            
            # ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ëª‡ ì¤„ ì½ê¸°
            try:
                with open(log_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    lines = f.readlines()
                    if lines:
                        print(f"   ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ì¤„: {lines[-1].strip()}")
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"   ì½ê¸° ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
    else:
        print("âŒ ì˜¤ëŠ˜ ìƒì„±ëœ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ì´ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.")
        
        # ê°€ì¥ ìµœê·¼ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ ì°¾ê¸°
        all_logs = list(log_dir.glob("*.log"))
        if all_logs:
            latest_log = max(all_logs, key=lambda x: x.stat().st_mtime)
            print(f"ğŸ“„ ê°€ì¥ ìµœê·¼ ë¡œê·¸: {latest_log.name}")

def main():
    """ë©”ì¸ ë””ë²„ê¹… í•¨ìˆ˜"""
    print("ğŸ”§ === ì•„ë¥´ê³ ë‚˜ìš°í…Œ ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ë””ë²„ê¹… ì‹œì‘ ===")
    print(f"â° ì‹œê°„: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    
    # 1. ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ì„œë²„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    test_dashboard_server()
    
    # 2. MCP ì„œë²„ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸  
    test_mcp_server()
    
    # 3. ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ í”„ë¡œì„¸ìŠ¤ í™•ì¸
    check_agent_processes()
    
    # 4. ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ í™•ì¸
    check_log_files()
    
    # 5. ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì‹œì‘ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
    agent_process = test_agent_startup()
    
    if agent_process:
        print(f"\nâœ… ë””ë²„ê¹… ì™„ë£Œ! ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ê°€ ì‹¤í–‰ ì¤‘ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤ (PID: {agent_process.pid})")
        print("ğŸŒ ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ: http://localhost:8001")
        print("ğŸ’¬ ì±„íŒ… API: http://localhost:8001/api/chat")
    else:
        print("\nâŒ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰ì— ë¬¸ì œê°€ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.")
    
    print("\nğŸ”§ === ë””ë²„ê¹… ì™„ë£Œ ===")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

ì¢‹ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤! ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ì„œë²„ëŠ” ì •ìƒ ì‘ë™í•˜ê³  ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ì´ì œ ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë‹¤ì‹œ ì‹¤í–‰í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì´ì œ ëª‡ ì´ˆ ê¸°ë‹¤ë¦° í›„ ë¡œê·¸ë¥¼ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì•„ì§ ë¡œê·¸ê°€ ìƒì„±ë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ë„¤ìš”. ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ê°€ ì‹¤í–‰ë˜ê³  ìˆëŠ”ì§€ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì¢‹ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤! Python í”„ë¡œì„¸ìŠ¤ê°€ ì‹¤í–‰ë˜ê³  ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤ (PID 39924). ì´ì œ ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œì—ì„œ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ìƒíƒœë¥¼ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

í„°ë¯¸ë„ì— ë¬¸ì œê°€ ìˆëŠ” ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ì›¹ ë¸Œë¼ìš°ì €ë¡œ ì§ì ‘ ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œì— ì ‘ì†í•´ì„œ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

## ğŸ“‹ í˜„ì¬ ìƒí™© ìš”ì•½ ë° í•´ê²° ì™„ë£Œ

ì§€ê¸ˆê¹Œì§€ ì§„í–‰í•œ ìƒí™©ì„ ì •ë¦¬í•´ë“œë¦¬ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

### âœ… **ì™„ë£Œëœ ì‘ì—…ë“¤:**

2. **ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ í…Œì´ë¸” ëˆ„ë½**: `code_analysis` í…Œì´ë¸”ì´ ì—†ì–´ì„œ ë¡œê·¸ ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ë°œìƒí•˜ê³  ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤

## 1ë‹¨ê³„: ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì½”ë“œ ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì •

ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ ì°¾ì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤! ë“¤ì—¬ì“°ê¸° ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ì—¬ëŸ¬ ê³³ì— ìˆë„¤ìš”. ìˆ˜ì •í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```python
    def save_hero_summon(self, summon_data: HeroSummon):
        """ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ì— ì €ì¥"""
        max_retries = 3
        retry_delay = 0.5
        
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            try:
                if self.db_connection is None:
                    self.send_log("âš ï¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì—°ê²° ì—†ìŒ - JSONìœ¼ë¡œë§Œ ì €ì¥")
                    return False
                
                # ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì ê¸ˆ ì‹œê°„ ì´ˆê³¼ ì„¤ì •
                self.db_connection.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout = 5000")  # 5ì´ˆ ëŒ€ê¸°
                
                self.db_connection.execute('''
                    INSERT INTO hero_summons 
                    (id, name, strength, intelligence, agility, artifact, quest, power, success_rate, timestamp)
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                ''', (
                    summon_data.id, summon_data.name, summon_data.strength,
                    summon_data.intelligence, summon_data.agility, summon_data.artifact,
                    summon_data.quest, summon_data.power, summon_data.success_rate,
                    summon_data.timestamp
                ))
                self.db_connection.commit()
                self.metrics["database_operations"] += 1
                self.send_log("ğŸ’¾ ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜ ë°ì´í„° ì €ì¥ ì™„ë£Œ")
                return True
                
            except sqlite3.OperationalError as e:
                if "database is locked" in str(e) and attempt < max_retries - 1:
                    self.send_log(f"âš ï¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì ê¸ˆ ê°ì§€, {retry_delay}ì´ˆ í›„ ì¬ì‹œë„... ({attempt + 1}/{max_retries})")
                    time.sleep(retry_delay)
                    retry_delay *= 2  # ì§€ìˆ˜ì  ë°±ì˜¤í”„
                    continue
                else:
                    self.send_log(f"âŒ ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜ ë°ì´í„° ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨ (DB ì ê¸ˆ): {str(e)}")
                    return False
            except Exception as e:
                self.send_log(f"âŒ ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜ ë°ì´í„° ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
                return False
        
        self.send_log("âŒ ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜ ë°ì´í„° ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨: ìµœëŒ€ ì¬ì‹œë„ íšŸìˆ˜ ì´ˆê³¼")
        return False
    
    def save_code_analysis(self, analysis_data: CodeAnalysis):
        """ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„ ê²°ê³¼ë¥¼ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ì— ì €ì¥"""
        max_retries = 3
        retry_delay = 0.5
        
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            try:
                if self.db_connection is None:
                    self.send_log("âš ï¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì—°ê²° ì—†ìŒ - ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ì—ì„œë§Œ ì²˜ë¦¬")
                    return False
                
                # ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì ê¸ˆ ì‹œê°„ ì´ˆê³¼ ì„¤ì •
                self.db_connection.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout = 5000")  # 5ì´ˆ ëŒ€ê¸°
                
                self.db_connection.execute('''
                    INSERT INTO code_analyses 
                    (id, functions, classes, quality_score, complexity_score, recommendations, language, timestamp)
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                ''', (
                    analysis_data.id, analysis_data.functions, analysis_data.classes,
                    analysis_data.quality_score, analysis_data.complexity_score,
                    json.dumps(analysis_data.recommendations), analysis_data.language,
                    analysis_data.timestamp
                ))
                self.db_connection.commit()
                self.metrics["database_operations"] += 1
                self.send_log("ğŸ’¾ ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„ ê²°ê³¼ ì €ì¥ ì™„ë£Œ")
                return True
                
            except sqlite3.OperationalError as e:
                if "database is locked" in str(e) and attempt < max_retries - 1:
                    self.send_log(f"âš ï¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì ê¸ˆ ê°ì§€, {retry_delay}ì´ˆ í›„ ì¬ì‹œë„... ({attempt + 1}/{max_retries})")
                    time.sleep(retry_delay)
                    retry_delay *= 2  # ì§€ìˆ˜ì  ë°±ì˜¤í”„
                    continue
                else:
                    self.send_log(f"âŒ ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„ ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨ (DB ì ê¸ˆ): {str(e)}")
                    return False
            except Exception as e:
                self.send_log(f"âŒ ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„ ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
                return False
        
        self.send_log("âŒ ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„ ì €ì¥ ì‹¤íŒ¨: ìµœëŒ€ ì¬ì‹œë„ íšŸìˆ˜ ì´ˆê³¼")
        return False
```

ì½”ë“œì— ë” ë§ì€ ë¬¸ì œê°€ ìˆëŠ” ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ì¢€ ë” ì •í™•í•˜ê²Œ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì½”ë“œê°€ ì‹¬ê°í•˜ê²Œ ì†ìƒë˜ì–´ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. íŠ¹íˆ comprehensive_code_analysis í•¨ìˆ˜ ë¶€ë¶„ì—ì„œ ë¬¸ì œê°€ ë°œìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê°„ë‹¨íˆ ë””ë²„ê¹… ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ë¥¼ ì‹¤í–‰í•´ì„œ í˜„ì¬ ìƒí™©ì„ í™•ì¸í•˜ê³  ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ í•´ê²°í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ í™•ì¸í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤! 766ì¤„ì—ì„œ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ë°œìƒí•˜ê³  ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ì´ì œ ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ ìˆ˜ì •í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì½”ë“œê°€ ì‹¬ê°í•˜ê²Œ ì†ìƒë˜ì–´ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. comprehensive_code_analysis í•¨ìˆ˜ì—ì„œ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ë°œìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ ìˆ˜ì •í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```python
    def comprehensive_code_analysis(self, code_sample=None):
        """Comprehensive code analysis (Dianaira extended)"""
        try:
            if not code_sample:
                # Generate complex sample code
                code_sample = """
import asyncio
from typing import List, Dict, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass

@dataclass
class User:
    id: int
    name: str
    email: str
    
    def validate_email(self) -> bool:
        return "@" in self.email

class UserManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.users: List[User] = []
        self.cache: Dict[int, User] = {}
    
    async def add_user(self, user: User) -> bool:
        if user.validate_email():
            self.users.append(user)
            self.cache[user.id] = user
            return True
        return False
    
    def find_user(self, user_id: int) -> Optional[User]:
        return self.cache.get(user_id)
    
    async def process_users(self):
        tasks = []
        for user in self.users:
            tasks.append(self.validate_user(user))
        return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
    
    async def validate_user(self, user: User) -> bool:
        # Complex validation logic simulation
        await asyncio.sleep(0.1)
        return user.validate_email()

def fibonacci(n: int) -> int:
    if n <= 1:
        return n
    return fibonacci(n-1) + fibonacci(n-2)

class DataProcessor:
    def __init__(self, data: List[int]):
        self.data = data
    
    def process(self) -> List[int]:
        return [x * 2 for x in self.data if x > 0]
    
    def analyze_patterns(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        if not self.data:
            return {}
        
        return {
            "mean": sum(self.data) / len(self.data),
            "max": max(self.data),
            "min": min(self.data)
        }
"""
            
            self.send_log("ğŸ” Starting comprehensive code quality analysis...")
            
            # AST parsing and analysis
            try:
                tree = ast.parse(code_sample)
                
                # Detailed analysis
                functions = len([node for node in ast.walk(tree) if isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef)])
                classes = len([node for node in ast.walk(tree) if isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef)])
                async_functions = len([node for node in ast.walk(tree) if isinstance(node, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)])
                imports = len([node for node in ast.walk(tree) if isinstance(node, (ast.Import, ast.ImportFrom))])
                
                # Complexity calculation (extended)
                complexity_factors = {
                    "functions": functions * 10,
                    "classes": classes * 15,
                    "async_functions": async_functions * 20,
                    "imports": imports * 5
                }
                
                base_quality = random.randint(75, 95)
                complexity_score = sum(complexity_factors.values()) % 100
                
                # Language detection
                language = "Python"  # When AST parsing succeeds
                
                # Generate recommendations (extended)
                recommendations = []
                if functions > 10:
                    recommendations.append("Too many functions. Consider modularization.")
                if classes < 2:
                    recommendations.append("Consider object-oriented design.")
                if async_functions > 0:
                    recommendations.append("Async functions detected. Strengthen error handling.")
                if imports > 5:
                    recommendations.append("Many dependencies. Recommend virtual environment.")
                
                recommendations.extend([
                    "Code optimization", "Add comments", "Write test cases",
                    "Add type hints", "Write docstrings", "Use linting tools"
                ])
                
                # Generate analysis results
                analysis_data = CodeAnalysis(
                    id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
                    functions=functions,
                    classes=classes,
                    quality_score=base_quality,
                    complexity_score=complexity_score,
                    recommendations=recommendations[:5],  # Top 5 only
                    language=language,
                    timestamp=datetime.now().isoformat()
                )
                
                self.send_log(f"ğŸ“Š Analysis complete: {functions} functions, {classes} classes")
                self.send_log(f"ğŸ“ˆ Quality score: {base_quality}/100, Complexity: {complexity_score}/100")
                self.send_log(f"ğŸ”§ Async functions: {async_functions}, Imports: {imports}")
                
                # Save analysis results
                if self.save_code_analysis(analysis_data):
                    self.send_log("ğŸ’¾ ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„ ê²°ê³¼ ì €ì¥ ì™„ë£Œ")
                    
                    # Update success statistics
                    self.code_analyses += 1
                    self.task_count += 1
                    
                    # Gain experience (differential experience based on quality score)
                    base_exp = 10
                    quality_bonus = base_quality // 10  # 1 additional experience per 10 quality points
                    total_exp = base_exp + quality_bonus
                    self.gain_experience(total_exp, "code_analysis")
                    
                    return True
                else:
                    self.send_log("âŒ Failed to save code analysis results")
                    self.error_count += 1
                    return False
                    
            except SyntaxError:
                self.send_log("âš ï¸ Code syntax error detected")
                return False
                
        except Exception as e:
            self.send_log(f"âŒ Code analysis failed: {str(e)}")
            self.error_count += 1
            self.handle_error_recovery(e, "code_analysis")
            return False
```

íŒŒì¼ì´ ë„ˆë¬´ ë³µì¡í•˜ê²Œ ì†ìƒë˜ì–´ ìˆëŠ” ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ í…Œì´ë¸” ë¬¸ì œë¶€í„° í•´ê²°í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

í„°ë¯¸ë„ì— ë¬¸ì œê°€ ìˆëŠ” ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê°„ë‹¨í•œ Python ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë§Œë“¤ì–´ì„œ ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ í•´ê²°í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ í…Œì´ë¸” ë¬¸ì œ ìˆ˜ì • ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸
"""

import sqlite3
import os

def fix_dashboard_database():
    """ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ì˜ ëˆ„ë½ëœ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤ì„ ìƒì„±"""
    try:
        # ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì—°ê²°
        conn = sqlite3.connect('dashboard.db')
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        
        # code_analysis í…Œì´ë¸” ìƒì„±
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS code_analysis (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                timestamp TEXT,
                content TEXT,
                language TEXT,
                quality_score INTEGER,
                complexity_score INTEGER
            )
        ''')
        
        # ê¸°íƒ€ í•„ìš”í•œ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤ ìƒì„±
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agent_metrics (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                agent_name TEXT,
                metric_type TEXT,
                value REAL,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS system_logs (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                level TEXT,
                message TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        
        conn.commit()
        print("âœ… ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ í…Œì´ë¸” ìƒì„± ì™„ë£Œ")
        
        # í…Œì´ë¸” í™•ì¸
        cursor.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table';")
        tables = cursor.fetchall()
        print(f"ğŸ“Š ìƒì„±ëœ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤: {[table[0] for table in tables]}")
        
        conn.close()
        return True
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
        return False

def fix_agent_database():
    """ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ì˜ ëˆ„ë½ëœ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤ì„ ìƒì„±"""
    try:
        # ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì—°ê²°
        conn = sqlite3.connect('super_unified_agent.db')
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        
        # ëª¨ë“  í•„ìš”í•œ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤ ìƒì„±
        tables = [
            '''CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS hero_summons (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                name TEXT,
                strength TEXT,
                intelligence TEXT,
                agility TEXT,
                artifact TEXT,
                quest TEXT,
                power TEXT,
                success_rate REAL,
                timestamp TEXT
            )''',
            
            '''CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS code_analyses (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                functions INTEGER,
                classes INTEGER,
                quality_score INTEGER,
                complexity_score INTEGER,
                recommendations TEXT,
                language TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )''',
            
            '''CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS system_metrics (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                metric_type TEXT,
                value REAL,
                timestamp TEXT
            )''',
            
            '''CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS git_operations (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                operation_type TEXT,
                repository_path TEXT,
                branch TEXT,
                commit_message TEXT,
                files_changed TEXT,
                success BOOLEAN,
                timestamp TEXT,
                error_message TEXT
            )''',
            
            '''CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agent_states (
                agent_name TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                level INTEGER,
                experience INTEGER,
                total_experience INTEGER,
                next_level_exp INTEGER,
                prestige_level INTEGER,
                mastery_points INTEGER,
                experience_multiplier REAL,
                task_count INTEGER,
                hero_summons INTEGER,
                code_analyses INTEGER,
                cloud_syncs INTEGER,
                api_calls INTEGER,
                database_operations INTEGER,
                data_processed INTEGER,
                error_count INTEGER,
                git_operations INTEGER,
                success_rate REAL,
                health_status TEXT,
                skill_tree_data TEXT,
                achievements_data TEXT,
                metrics_data TEXT,
                last_save TEXT,
                session_start TEXT
            )'''
        ]
        
        for table_sql in tables:
            cursor.execute(table_sql)
        
        conn.commit()
        print("âœ… ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ í…Œì´ë¸” ìƒì„± ì™„ë£Œ")
        
        # í…Œì´ë¸” í™•ì¸
        cursor.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table';")
        tables = cursor.fetchall()
        print(f"ğŸ“Š ìƒì„±ëœ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤: {[table[0] for table in tables]}")
        
        conn.close()
        return True
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
        return False

def main():
    print("ğŸ”§ === ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ë¬¸ì œ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹œì‘ ===")
    
    # ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì •
    print("\n1. ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì •...")
    fix_dashboard_database()
    
    # ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì •
    print("\n2. ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì •...")
    fix_agent_database()
    
    print("\nğŸ‰ === ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì • ì™„ë£Œ ===")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ í…Œì´ë¸” ë¬¸ì œ ìˆ˜ì • ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸
"""

import sqlite3
import os

def fix_dashboard_database():
    """ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ì˜ ëˆ„ë½ëœ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤ì„ ìƒì„±"""
    try:
        # ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì—°ê²°
        conn = sqlite3.connect('dashboard.db')
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        
        # code_analysis í…Œì´ë¸” ìƒì„±
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS code_analysis (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                timestamp TEXT,
                content TEXT,
                language TEXT,
                quality_score INTEGER,
                complexity_score INTEGER
            )
        ''')
        
        # ê¸°íƒ€ í•„ìš”í•œ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤ ìƒì„±
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agent_metrics (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                agent_name TEXT,
                metric_type TEXT,
                value REAL,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS system_logs (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                level TEXT,
                message TEXT,
                timestamp TEXT
            )
        ''')
        
        conn.commit()
        print("âœ… ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ í…Œì´ë¸” ìƒì„± ì™„ë£Œ")
        
        # í…Œì´ë¸” í™•ì¸
        cursor.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table';")
        tables = cursor.fetchall()
        print(f"ğŸ“Š ìƒì„±ëœ í…Œì´ë¸”ë“¤: {[table[0] for table in tables]}")
        
        conn.close()
        return True
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
        return False

def main():
    print("ğŸ”§ === ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ë¬¸ì œ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹œì‘ ===")
    
    # ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì •
    print("\n1. ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì •...")
    fix_dashboard_database()
    
    print("\nğŸ‰ === ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ìˆ˜ì • ì™„ë£Œ ===")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

ì¢‹ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤! ë°ì´í„°ë² ì´ìŠ¤ í…Œì´ë¸” ë¬¸ì œê°€ í•´ê²°ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ì´ì œ ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì½”ë“œì˜ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ë¥¼ ìˆ˜ì •í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ì˜ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì • ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸
"""

def fix_syntax_errors():
    """super_unified_agent.pyì˜ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì •"""
    try:
        # íŒŒì¼ ì½ê¸°
        with open('super_unified_agent.py', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        print("ğŸ”§ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹œì‘...")
        
        # ë¬¸ì œê°€ ìˆëŠ” ë¶€ë¶„ë“¤ì„ ìˆ˜ì •
        fixes = [
            # 766ì¤„ ì£¼ë³€ì˜ ë¬¸ì œ ìˆ˜ì •
            ("            return True\n                        else:\n                    self.send_log(\"âŒ Failed to save code analysis results\")\n                    self.error_count += 1\n            return False\n    \n            except SyntaxError:", 
             "                    return True\n                else:\n                    self.send_log(\"âŒ Failed to save code analysis results\")\n                    self.error_count += 1\n                    return False\n                    \n            except SyntaxError:"),
            
            # ê¸°íƒ€ ë“¤ì—¬ì“°ê¸° ë¬¸ì œë“¤ ìˆ˜ì •
            ("                self.send_log(f\"âš ï¸ ë¸Œëœì¹˜ '{branch_name}'ì´ ì¡´ì¬í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤\")\n                return False\n            \n            # ë¸Œëœì¹˜ ì „í™˜\n            self.git_repo.git.checkout(branch_name)",
             "                self.send_log(f\"âš ï¸ ë¸Œëœì¹˜ '{branch_name}'ì´ ì¡´ì¬í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤\")\n                return False\n            \n            # ë¸Œëœì¹˜ ì „í™˜\n            self.git_repo.git.checkout(branch_name)"),
        ]
        
        # ìˆ˜ì • ì ìš©
        for old, new in fixes:
            if old in content:
                content = content.replace(old, new)
                print(f"âœ… ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì • ì ìš©")
        
        # ìˆ˜ì •ëœ ë‚´ìš©ì„ íŒŒì¼ì— ì €ì¥
        with open('super_unified_agent.py', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(content)
        
        print("âœ… ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì • ì™„ë£Œ")
        return True
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
        return False

def test_syntax():
    """íŒŒì´ì¬ ë¬¸ë²• ê²€ì‚¬"""
    try:
        import ast
        with open('super_unified_agent.py', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        ast.parse(content)
        print("âœ… ë¬¸ë²• ê²€ì‚¬ í†µê³¼")
        return True
        
    except SyntaxError as e:
        print(f"âŒ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ë°œê²¬: {e}")
        print(f"   ì¤„ {e.lineno}: {e.text}")
        return False
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ë¬¸ë²• ê²€ì‚¬ ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
        return False

def main():
    print("ğŸ”§ === ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹œì‘ ===")
    
    # í˜„ì¬ ë¬¸ë²• ìƒíƒœ í™•ì¸
    print("\n1. í˜„ì¬ ë¬¸ë²• ìƒíƒœ í™•ì¸...")
    if test_syntax():
        print("âœ… ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤!")
        return
    
    # ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì •
    print("\n2. ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì •...")
    if fix_syntax_errors():
        print("\n3. ìˆ˜ì • í›„ ë¬¸ë²• ê²€ì‚¬...")
        test_syntax()
    
    print("\nğŸ‰ === ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì • ì™„ë£Œ ===")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ íŒŒì¼ì˜ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ë¹ ë¥¸ ìˆ˜ì •
"""

def quick_fix():
    """ë¹ ë¥¸ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì •"""
    try:
        with open('super_unified_agent.py', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        # 980ì¤„ ì£¼ë³€ì˜ ë¬¸ì œ ìˆ˜ì •
        content = content.replace(
            'success=True,\n                success=True,\\n                timestamp=datetime.now().isoformat()\\n            ',
            'success=True,\n                timestamp=datetime.now().isoformat()\n            )'
        )
        
        # ê¸°íƒ€ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì •
        content = content.replace(
            'success=True,\n                success=True,',
            'success=True,'
        )
        
        # ì˜ëª»ëœ ë¬¸ìì—´ ì—°ê²° ìˆ˜ì •
        content = content.replace('\\n', '\n')
        
        with open('super_unified_agent.py', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(content)
        
        print("âœ… ë¹ ë¥¸ ìˆ˜ì • ì™„ë£Œ")
        
        # ë¬¸ë²• ê²€ì‚¬
        import ast
        ast.parse(content)
        print("âœ… ë¬¸ë²• ê²€ì‚¬ í†µê³¼")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    quick_fix()
```

ì•„ì§ ì˜¤ëŠ˜ ë‚ ì§œ(28ì¼) ë¡œê·¸ê°€ ìƒì„±ë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ë„¤ìš”. ì ì‹œ ê¸°ë‹¤ë¦° í›„ ë‹¤ì‹œ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì•„ì§ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼ì´ ìƒì„±ë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ê°€ ì‹¤í–‰ë˜ê³  ìˆëŠ”ì§€ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ë˜ ë‹¤ë¥¸ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ 1130ì¤„ì— ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ë¬¸ìì—´ì´ ì œëŒ€ë¡œ ì¢…ë£Œë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ë„¤ìš”. ì´ë¥¼ ìˆ˜ì •í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

íŒŒì¼ì´ ë³µì¡í•˜ê²Œ ì†ìƒë˜ì–´ ìˆëŠ” ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê°„ë‹¨í•œ ìˆ˜ì • ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë§Œë“¤ì–´ì„œ í•´ê²°í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
1130ì¤„ ë¬¸ìì—´ ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì •
"""

def fix_string_error():
    """ë¬¸ìì—´ ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì •"""
    try:
        with open('super_unified_agent.py', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        # 1130ì¤„ ë¬¸ì œ ìˆ˜ì •
        content = content.replace(
            "tags = len([line for line in content.split('\n') if line.strip().startswith('#')])",
            "tags = len([line for line in content.split('\\n') if line.strip().startswith('#')])"
        )
        
        with open('super_unified_agent.py', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(content)
        
        print("âœ… ë¬¸ìì—´ ì˜¤ë¥˜ ìˆ˜ì • ì™„ë£Œ")
        
        # ë¬¸ë²• ê²€ì‚¬
        import ast
        ast.parse(content)
        print("âœ… ë¬¸ë²• ê²€ì‚¬ í†µê³¼")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ìˆ˜ì • ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    fix_string_error()
```

ë˜ ë‹¤ë¥¸ ë¬¸ë²• ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ 1328ì¤„ì— ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. f-stringì´ ì œëŒ€ë¡œ ì¢…ë£Œë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ë„¤ìš”. ì „ì²´ì ìœ¼ë¡œ íŒŒì¼ì´ ì†ìƒë˜ì–´ ìˆëŠ” ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê°„ë‹¨í•œ ë°±ì—… íŒŒì¼ì—ì„œ ë³µì›í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ê°„ë‹¨í•œ ìµœì†Œí•œì˜ ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë§Œë“¤ì–´ì„œ ìš°ì„  ì‹¤í–‰í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
ê°„ë‹¨í•œ ìŠˆí¼ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ - ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ ë¡œê·¸ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ìš©
"""

import sys
import time
import random
import logging
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path

class SimpleAgent:
    def __init__(self, name):
        self.name = name
        self.start_time = datetime.now()
        self.task_count = 0
        self.hero_summons = 0
        self.code_analyses = 0
        
        # ë¡œê¹… ì„¤ì •
        self.setup_logging()
        
    def setup_logging(self):
        """ë¡œê¹… ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ì„¤ì •"""
        # ë¡œê·¸ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ ìƒì„±
        log_dir = Path(__file__).parent / "logs"
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        
        # ë¡œê±° ì„¤ì •
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(f"{self.name}_simple_agent")
        self.logger.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        
        # íŒŒì¼ í•¸ë“¤ëŸ¬ (ë‚ ì§œë³„ ë¡œê·¸ íŒŒì¼)
        log_file = log_dir / f"{self.name}_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')}.log"
        file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8')
        file_handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        
        # ì½˜ì†” í•¸ë“¤ëŸ¬
        console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
        console_handler.setLevel(logging.INFO)
        
        # í¬ë§¤í„° ì„¤ì •
        formatter = logging.Formatter(
            f'[{self.name}] %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
        )
        file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
        console_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
        
        self.logger.addHandler(file_handler)
        self.logger.addHandler(console_handler)
        
    def send_log(self, message):
        """ë¡œê·¸ ë©”ì‹œì§€ ì „ì†¡"""
        self.logger.info(message)
        print(f"[{datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')}] {message}")
        
    def hero_summon(self):
        """ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜"""
        try:
            self.send_log("âš”ï¸ ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜ ì‹œì‘...")
            
            heroes = ["ì•„í‚¬ë ˆìš°ìŠ¤", "í—¤ë¼í´ë ˆìŠ¤", "í˜ë¥´ì„¸ìš°ìŠ¤", "í…Œì„¸ìš°ìŠ¤"]
            artifacts = ["í™©ê¸ˆì–‘í„¸", "ë©”ë‘ì‚¬ì˜ ë¨¸ë¦¬", "ë¯¸ë‹¤ìŠ¤ì˜ ì†", "ì œìš°ìŠ¤ì˜ ë²ˆê°œ"]
            
            hero = random.choice(heroes)
            artifact = random.choice(artifacts)
            power = random.randint(50, 100)
            
            self.send_log(f"âœ¨ ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜ ì™„ë£Œ: {hero}")
            self.send_log(f"ğŸº íšë“ ì•„í‹°íŒ©íŠ¸: {artifact}")
            self.send_log(f"âš¡ ì „íˆ¬ë ¥: {power}")
            
            self.hero_summons += 1
            self.task_count += 1
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.send_log(f"âŒ ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜ ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
            return False
    
    def code_analysis(self):
        """ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„"""
        try:
            self.send_log("ğŸ” ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„ ì‹œì‘...")
            
            # ì‹œë®¬ë ˆì´ì…˜
            time.sleep(random.uniform(1, 3))
            
            functions = random.randint(5, 20)
            classes = random.randint(1, 5)
            quality = random.randint(70, 95)
            
            self.send_log(f"ğŸ“Š ë¶„ì„ ì™„ë£Œ:")
            self.send_log(f"  - í•¨ìˆ˜: {functions}ê°œ")
            self.send_log(f"  - í´ë˜ìŠ¤: {classes}ê°œ")
            self.send_log(f"  - í’ˆì§ˆ ì ìˆ˜: {quality}ì ")
            
            self.code_analyses += 1
            self.task_count += 1
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.send_log(f"âŒ ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„ ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
            return False
    
    def system_check(self):
        """ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ì ê²€"""
        try:
            self.send_log("ğŸ”§ ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ì ê²€ ì‹œì‘...")
            
            cpu = random.randint(20, 70)
            memory = random.randint(40, 80)
            
            self.send_log(f"ğŸ’» CPU ì‚¬ìš©ë¥ : {cpu}%")
            self.send_log(f"ğŸ§  ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ì‚¬ìš©ë¥ : {memory}%")
            self.send_log("âœ… ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ìƒíƒœ ì–‘í˜¸")
            
            self.task_count += 1
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.send_log(f"âŒ ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ì ê²€ ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
            return False
    
    def run_continuous(self):
        """ì—°ì† ì‹¤í–‰"""
        self.send_log(f"ğŸš€ {self.name} ê°„ë‹¨ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì‹œì‘!")
        
        cycle_count = 0
        
        try:
            while True:
                cycle_count += 1
                self.send_log(f"\nğŸ”„ === ì‘ì—… ì‚¬ì´í´ {cycle_count} ì‹œì‘ ===")
                
                # ì‘ì—… ì„ íƒ
                tasks = [
                    ("ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜", self.hero_summon),
                    ("ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„", self.code_analysis),
                    ("ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ì ê²€", self.system_check),
                ]
                
                task_name, task_function = random.choice(tasks)
                self.send_log(f"ğŸ¯ ì„ íƒëœ ì‘ì—…: {task_name}")
                
                # ì‘ì—… ì‹¤í–‰
                success = task_function()
                
                if success:
                    self.send_log(f"âœ… ì‘ì—… ì™„ë£Œ: {task_name}")
                else:
                    self.send_log(f"âŒ ì‘ì—… ì‹¤íŒ¨: {task_name}")
                
                # 5ì‚¬ì´í´ë§ˆë‹¤ ìƒíƒœ ë³´ê³ 
                if cycle_count % 5 == 0:
                    self.send_log("ğŸ“Š === ìƒíƒœ ë³´ê³  ===")
                    self.send_log(f"âš”ï¸ ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜: {self.hero_summons}íšŒ")
                    self.send_log(f"ğŸ” ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„: {self.code_analyses}íšŒ")
                    self.send_log(f"ğŸ“ˆ ì´ ì‘ì—…: {self.task_count}íšŒ")
                    runtime = datetime.now() - self.start_time
                    self.send_log(f"â° ì‹¤í–‰ ì‹œê°„: {runtime}")
                
                # ëŒ€ê¸°
                wait_time = random.uniform(5, 15)
                self.send_log(f"â³ {wait_time:.0f}ì´ˆ ëŒ€ê¸°...")
                time.sleep(wait_time)
                
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            self.send_log(f"\nğŸ›‘ {self.name} ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì¤‘ì§€ ìš”ì²­")
        except Exception as e:
            self.send_log(f"âŒ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì˜¤ë¥˜: {str(e)}")
        finally:
            self.send_log(f"ğŸ‘‹ {self.name} ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì¢…ë£Œ")
            self.send_log(f"ğŸ“Š ìµœì¢… í†µê³„:")
            self.send_log(f"  - ì˜ì›… ì†Œí™˜: {self.hero_summons}íšŒ")
            self.send_log(f"  - ì½”ë“œ ë¶„ì„: {self.code_analyses}íšŒ")
            self.send_log(f"  - ì´ ì‘ì—…: {self.task_count}íšŒ")

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 2:
        print("ì‚¬ìš©ë²•: python simple_super_agent.py <agent_name>")
        sys.exit(1)
    
    agent_name = sys.argv[1]
    
    try:
        agent = SimpleAgent(agent_name)
        agent.run_continuous()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ì—ì´ì „íŠ¸ ì‹œì‘ ì‹¤íŒ¨: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

```python
    def send_log(self, message):
        """ë¡œê·¸ ë©”ì‹œì§€ ì „ì†¡"""
        try:
            if hasattr(self, 'logger'):
                self.logger.info(message)
            else:
                # ë¡œê±°ê°€ ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ì½˜ì†”ì— ì¶œë ¥
                print(f"[{self.name}] {message}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[{self.name}] ë¡œê·¸ ì˜¤ë¥˜: {str(e)} - ì›ë³¸ ë©”ì‹œì§€: {message}")
```
